```python
readings = data["readings"][0]
print(len(readings))
temp = []
for sample in readings:
  if sample["sensor_id"]==1:
    temp.append(int(sample["value"]))

print(temp)
temp_short = temp[610:800]
x_short = []
for i in range(len(temp_short)):
  x_short.append(i)

plt.scatter(x_short, temp_short)

m, b= polyfit(x_short, temp_short)
x_line = [0, len(x_short)]
y_line = []
for i in x_line:
  y_line.append(m*i*b)
plt.plot(x_line, y_line)
a1, a2, a3 = polyfit(x_short, temp_short, 2)
y_model_quad = []
for i in x_short:
    y_model_quad.append(a1*i**2 + a2*i + a3)
plt.show()
```

**Fig. 1** Proof
